id="u_0_5">Remove</button><div class="_4juw">To help personalise content, tailor and measure adverts and provide a safer experience, we use cookies. Learn more, including about available controls: <a class="_5l9y" href="https://www.facebook.com/policies/cookies/" id="cpn-pv-link" data-pv="2" target="_blank">Cookies Policy</a>.</div></div></div><div id="globalContainer" class="uiContextualLayerParent"><div class="fb_content clearfix " id="content" role="main"><div class="_r6n _3m9" id="content"><div class="clearfix _r6o" id="cs-header"><div class="_r6p"><a class="_r6q" href="/communitystandards/?fb_home" title="Home"><i class="img sp_HBeqgA9O27P sx_6f6e08"></i></a><a class="_r6s" href="/communitystandards/"><span>Community Standards</span></a></div></div><div class="_w_k"><div class="_4-u2 _w_j _4-u8"><div class="_w_l"></div><div class="_w_m"><div class="_5aj7"><div class="_4bl9"> Our mission is to give people the power to share and make the world more open and connected. Every day, people come to Facebook to share their stories, see the world through the eyes of others and connect with friends and causes. The conversations that happen on Facebook reflect the diversity of a community of more than one billion people. <br /><br /> We want people to feel safe when using Facebook. For that reason, we&#039;ve developed a set of Community Standards, outlined below. These policies will help you understand what type of sharing is allowed on Facebook, and what type of content may be reported to us and removed. Because of the diversity of our global community, please bear in mind that something that may be disagreeable or disturbing to you may not violate our Community Standards. </div><div class="_4bl7 _w_p"><i class="_w_o img sp_JpGEe8QWY_S sx_032b9b"></i><a class="_42ft _4jy0 _55pi _2agf _w_n _4jy3 _4jy2 selected _51sy" role="button" href="/communitystandards/?letter" id="helping-to-keep-you-safe"><div class="_w_m"><div class="_5aj7 _2auw" id="helping-to-keep-you-safe"><div class="_4bl9">Helping to keep you safe</div><div class="_4bl7 _2aux _w_p"><a href="#cs-header">Back to top<i class="_2auy img sp_Q5CmT_z3RST sx_b0015c"></i></a></div></div><div class="clearfix _ikh"><div class="_4bl7 _2auz"><i class="img sp_JpGEe8QWY_S id="encouraging-respectful-behavior"><div class="_4bl9">Encouraging respectful behaviour</div><div class="_4bl7 _2aux _w_p"><a href="#cs-header">Back to top<i class="_2auy img sp_Q5CmT_z3RST class="_4bl7 _2aux _w_p"><a href="#cs-header">Back to top<i class="_2auy img sp_Q5CmT_z3RST sx_b0015c"></i></a></div></div><div class="clearfix _ikh"><div class="_4bl7 _2auz"><i class="img _2auw" id="protecting-your-intellectual-property"><div class="_4bl9">Protecting your intellectual property</div><div class="_4bl7 _2aux _w_p"><a href="#cs-header">Back to top<i class="_2auy img sp_Q5CmT_z3RST sx_b0015c"></i></a></div></div><div class="clearfix _ikh"><div class="_4bl7 _2auz"><i class="img sp_JpGEe8QWY_S sx_63db60"></i></div><div class="_4bl9"><div id="u_0_0"><span class="img _55ym _55yq _55yo _3kks" aria-busy="true" role="progressbar" aria-valuemin="0" aria-valuemax="100" aria-valuetext="Loading..."></span></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="_w_q"><div class="_w_j"><div class="_w_m"><div class="_2auw _3ma">Reporting abuse</div><div class="_5aj7"><div class="_4bl9 _w_r"> Our global community is growing every day, and we strive to welcome people to an environment that is free from abusive content. To do this, we rely on people like you. If you see something on Facebook that you believe violates our terms, <a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/www/181495968648557">please report it to us</a>. We have dedicated teams working around the world to review things you report to help make sure Facebook remains safe. <br /><br /> Governments also sometimes ask us to remove content that violates local laws but does not violate our Community Standards. If after careful legal review we find that the content is illegal under local law, then we may make it unavailable only in the relevant country or territory. <br /><br /> Please bear the following in mind: <br /><br /><ul class="_p7q"><li> We may take action whenever something violates the Community Standards outlined here. </li><li> We may ask Page owners to associate their name and Facebook Profile with a Page that contains cruel and insensitive content, even if that content does not violate our policies. </li><li> Reporting something doesn&#039;t guarantee that it will be removed because it may not violate our policies. </li><li> Our content reviewers will look to you for information about why a post may violate our policies. If you report content, please tell us why the content should be removed (e.g. is it nudity or hate speech?) so that we can send it to the right person for review. </li><li> Our review decisions may occasionally change after receiving additional context about specific posts or after seeing new, violating content appearing on a Page or Facebook Profile. </li><li> The number of reports does not impact whether something will be removed. We never remove content simply because it has been reported a number of times. </li><li> The consequences for violating our Community Standards vary depending on the severity of the violation and the person&#039;s history on Facebook. For instance, we may warn someone for a first violation, but if we continue to see further violations we may restrict a person&#039;s ability to post on Facebook or ban the person from Facebook.</li></ul><br /> Not all disagreeable or disturbing content violates our Community Standards. For this reason, we offer you the ability to customise and control what you see by unfollowing, blocking and hiding the posts, people, Pages and applications you don&#039;t want to see â and we encourage you to use these controls to better personalise your experience. <a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/212722115425932">Learn more</a>. People also often resolve issues they have about a piece of content by simply getting in touch with the person who posted it. We&#039;ve created <a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/www/128548343894719">tools</a> for you to communicate directly with other people when you&#039;re unhappy with posts, photos or other content you see on Facebook. </div><div class="_4bl7 _w_p"><a class="_42ft _4jy0 _55pi _2agf _w_n _4jy3 _4jy2 selected _51sy" role="button" href="/help/181495968648557?ref=community_standards"
